---
title: "史拉蟾"

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 22pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(192,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 22.0000pt">史拉蟾</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 22pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(192,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 22.0000pt">Slaadi</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> 在混沌海Limbo的永恒混乱里，丛林、草甸、废墟和孤岛转化为躁动的水、火、土、气。这个环境恶劣的位面中，最初的住民是看似蛤蟆的史拉蟾。史拉蟾没有纪律观念也没有寻常的阶级观，不过弱小的史拉蟾还是会在性命威胁下服从更强的个体。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> </span>***<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">产卵石The Spawning Stone。</span>***<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">很久以前，魔冢主宰奇点Primus制造了一块几何复形的巨石并灌以法则之力。随后便将之投入混沌海中任其漂泊，相信这块石头能控制该位面的混乱并阻止混乱传播到其他位面。随着石头的能量成长，其存在使守序居民（如魔冢和吉斯泽莱人）殖民混沌海成为可能。然而，奇点的造物有一个没预见到的副作用：被这块石头吸收的混沌能量孵育了后来被称为史拉蟾的恐怖存在。因此先贤们才以“奇点的大规模造物”指代“产卵石”。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">  
</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> 史拉蟾扫灭了魔冢在混沌海的每一处殖民地。作为纯粹混乱的生物，史拉蟾嫌恶并攻击视野所及的魔冢。虽然如此，奇点却站在自己的造物一边，既不把史拉蟾当作威胁，也不选择无视它们。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> </span>***<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">诞生与进化Birth and Transformation。</span>***<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">史拉蟾的繁殖循环十分骇人。史拉蟾的繁衍需要在类人生物体内强制植卵或者使他们感染一种叫混沌噬菌体chaos phage的畸变型疾病。各个颜色的史拉蟾以不同的方式繁衍或转化，史拉红蟾产出史拉蓝蟾和史拉绿蟾，史拉蓝蟾产出史拉红蟾和史拉绿蟾。史拉绿蟾通过终生的进化循环成长为更强的史拉灰蟾和史拉亡蟾。在每个进化阶段，史拉蟾都会保留其记忆。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> </span>***<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">变形生物Shapechangers。</span>***<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">一些史拉蟾能变成孵育它们的类人生物母体。而这些史拉蟾会以伪装的姿态回到主物质位面惹是生非。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 15pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">史拉蟾蝌蚪Slaad Tadpole</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Cambria; mso-hansi-font-family: Cambria; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">微型异怪，混乱中立</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Cambria; COLOR: rgb(99,36,35); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold"> </span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">护甲等级：</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">12</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">  
</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">生命值：</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">10</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">（</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">4d4</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">）</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">  
</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">速度：</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">30</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">尺</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Cambria; COLOR: rgb(99,36,35); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold"> </span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">力量</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">7</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">（</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">-2</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">）</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">敏捷</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">（</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">魅力</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">3</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">（</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">-4</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">）</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Cambria; COLOR: rgb(99,36,35); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold"> </span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">技能：隐匿</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">+4</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">  
</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">伤害抗性：强酸，寒冷，火焰，闪电，雷鸣</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">  
</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">感官：黑暗视觉</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">60</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">尺，被动察觉</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">7</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">  
</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">语言：懂史拉蟾语但不能说</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">  
</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">挑战等级：</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">1/8</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">（</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">25 XP</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">）</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Cambria; COLOR: rgb(99,36,35); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold"> </span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';"> </span>***<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">魔法抗性</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">Magic Resistance</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">。</span>***<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">史拉蟾为抵抗法术和其他魔法效应而作的豁免检定具有优势。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">动作</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';"> </span>***<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">啃咬</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">Bite</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">。</span>****<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">近战武器攻击：</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">命中</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">+4</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">，触及</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">5</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">尺，单一目标。</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">命中：</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">4</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">（</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">1d4+2</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">）点穿刺伤害。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">变体：史拉蟾之心</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman'; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 黑体;">Variant: Slaad Control Gems</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">既然史拉蟾诞生自产卵石，而这石头则以魔法将自身的碎片植入史拉蟾的大脑。碎片看起来像是魔法宝石并且大小和形状约略像人类小孩的拳头。宝石的颜色与该史拉蟾相对应。而另一个生物可以用魔法唤出史拉蟾之心借以降服该史拉蟾。史拉蟾必须服从任何拥有该宝石的人。如果史拉蟾之心被毁，则该史拉蟾就再也不能以此方式被控制。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">  
</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">并非从产卵石诞生的史拉蟾脑内并无宝石，只是一旦其与产卵石有接触便会以此为契机生成宝石。混沌海的史拉蟾族被产卵石吸引着，所以大多都有这宝石。脑内有史拉蟾之心的史拉蟾有如下额外特质。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"> </span>***<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">支配宝石</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">Control Gem</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">。</span>***<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">植入史拉蟾脑内的是一个魔法控制宝石。史拉蟾必须遵从任何持有该宝石者，且在被支配时免疫魅惑。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">  
</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">某些特定的法术可以用来唤取宝石。如果史拉蟾对</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">禁锢术</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">imprisonment</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">的豁免失败，则此法术可以将宝石转移到施法者摊开的手上而不是禁锢史拉蟾。</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">祈愿术</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">wish</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">对史拉蟾作用时，也可以措辞谨慎地唤取该宝石。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">  
</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">施展在史拉蟾身上的</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">高等复原术</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">greater restoration</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">会摧毁史拉蟾之心而不伤及史拉蟾。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">  
</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">拥有感知（医药）熟练项的人可以从失能的史拉蟾身上取走史拉蟾之心。每次尝试需要</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">1</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">分钟不受打扰的工作，以及成功通过一次</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">DC 20</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">的感知（医药）检定。每次失败的尝试都会对该史拉蟾造成</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">22</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">（</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">4d10</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt">）点心灵伤害。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">史拉红蟾</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman'; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 黑体;">Red Slaad</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> 当史拉红蟾的爪子击中类人生物时，它可以从爪下的腺体把卵植入对方体内。卵在宿主体内孵化，最终形成史拉蝌蚪。这种蝌蚪从宿主体内吃出一条通路，从遗体上获得养分，然后寻找其他能找到的鲜肉。2d12小时后，史拉蝌蚪进化为成熟体史拉蓝蟾或者如果宿主有能力施展3环或更环阶法术时，还会成长为史拉绿蟾。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 15pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">史拉红蟾Red Slaad</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Cambria; mso-hansi-font-family: Cambria; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">大型异怪，混乱中立</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Cambria; COLOR: rgb(99,36,35); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold"> </span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">护甲等级：</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">14</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">（天生护甲）</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">生命值：</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">93</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">（</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">11d10+33</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">）</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">速度：</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">30</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">尺</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">1d8+3</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">）点穿刺伤害。如果目标是一类人生物，则其必须成功通过一次</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">DC 14</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">的体质豁免否则感染疾病</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';"></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">史拉蟾微卵</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">minuscule slaad egg</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">  
</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">一个类人生物一次只能携带一枚史拉蟾卵。三个月后，卵移动到胸腔，并孵化形成史拉蟾蝌蚪。诞生前</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">24</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">小时，宿主开始感觉不适，因此速度减半，其攻击检定、属性检定和豁免检定具有劣势。诞生时，蝌蚪吃穿生命器官并在</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">1</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">轮内遁出体外，并在此过程中杀死宿主。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">  
</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">若疾病在蝌蚪出现前治愈，未诞生的史拉蟾将就此被解离。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">史拉蓝蟾</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman'; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 黑体;">Blue Slaad</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> 史拉蓝蟾手背突起的骨钩会让被其挠伤的类人生物感染一种可怕的畸变型疾病。这种称为混沌噬菌体的感染物，会把受害者变成成熟体史拉红蟾或者如果宿主有能力施展3环或更环阶法术时，还会成长为史拉绿蟾。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 15pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">史拉蓝蟾Blue Slaad</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">12</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">（</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">2d6+5</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">）点挥砍伤害。如果目标是一类人生物，则其必须成功通过一次</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">DC 15</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">的体质豁免否则感染称为混沌噬菌体</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">chaos phage</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">的疾病。受感染的目标无法恢复生命值，且其生命值上限每经过</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">24</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">小时减损</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">10</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">（</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">3d6</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">）。如果该疾病将目标的生命值上限降至</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">0</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">，则该目标立即被转化为一只史拉红蟾，或者如果目标有能力施展</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">3</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">环或更环阶法术时则转化为一只史拉绿蟾。只有法术</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">祈愿术</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">wish</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">可以将该转化逆转。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">史拉绿蟾</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman'; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 黑体;">Green Slaad</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> 史拉绿蟾拥有令人惊异的高智能和天生施法能力，还能变成类人生物的样子。如果它从类人生物宿主中孵出，通常还会继承其宿主的外观形态。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">  
</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> 史拉绿蟾会在其生命中某个不可知的时点解密魔法，并立即且永久的进化为史拉灰蟾。而解密这项知识可能需要数年甚至数十年的时间。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 15pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">史拉绿蟾Green Slaad</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Cambria; mso-hansi-font-family: Cambria; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">大型异怪（变形生物），混乱中立</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Cambria; COLOR: rgb(99,36,35); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold"> </span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">护甲等级：</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">16</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">（天生护甲）</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">生命值：</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">127</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">（</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">15d10+45</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">）</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">速度：</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">30</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">尺</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';"> </span>***<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">天生施法</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">Innate Spellcasting</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">。</span>***<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">史拉蟾天生施法属性为魅力（法术豁免</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">DC 12</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">）。该史拉蟾天生可施展如下法术，且无需任何相应的材料成分：</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">随意：</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">侦测魔法</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">detect magic</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">，侦测思想</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">detect thoughts</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">，</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">

mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">命中：</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">10</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">（</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';">3d6</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">）点火焰伤害。火焰将点燃所有未被着装或携带的可燃物件。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">史拉灰蟾</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman'; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 黑体;">Gray Slaad</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> 在混沌海外侧，史拉灰蟾是它们的主人史拉亡蟾的意志延伸。史拉灰蟾跑到主物质位面执行散播死亡的差事。它们还会运用巨剑，并用自己天生的法术使之得到强化。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">  
</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> 史拉灰蟾在吃掉史拉亡蟾完整的遗体后将立即进化为史拉亡蟾。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Cambria; COLOR: rgb(99,36,35); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold"> </span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">技能：奥秘</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">+5</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">，察觉</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">+7</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">伤害抗性：强酸，寒冷，火焰，闪电，雷鸣</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">感官：盲视</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">60</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">尺，黑暗视觉</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">60</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">尺，被动察觉</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">17</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">语言：史拉蟾语，心灵感应</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">60</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">尺</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">挑战等级：</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">9</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">（</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">5,000 XP</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">）</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 'STHeiti light';"> </span>***<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">变形生物</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">Shapechanger</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">。</span>***<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">史拉蟾用一个动作变形小型或中型体型的类人生物，或以同样的动作变回其真实形态。除体型外，它在每个形态下的所有其他资料不变。其着装或携带的任何装备也不会随之改变。史拉蟾死亡时将恢复其真实形态。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-hansi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">史拉亡蟾</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman'; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 黑体;">Death Slaad</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> 史拉亡蟾会从伤害他人中寻找暴虐的快感，它们身上弥漫着来自负能量位面的气息，是腐臭混沌的邪恶典范。它们奴役麾下的史拉红、蓝蟾手下们入侵其他位面以壮大自身种族。入侵中幸存的类人生物则成为新史拉蟾的苗床。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 15pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">史拉亡蟾Death Slaad</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Cambria; mso-hansi-font-family: Cambria; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">中型异怪（变形生物），混乱邪恶</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Cambria; COLOR: rgb(99,36,35); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold"> </span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-spacerun: 'yes';"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">护甲等级：</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">18</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">（天生护甲）</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">生命值：</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">170</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">（</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">20d8+80</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">）</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">速度：</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">30</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">尺</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">技能：奥秘</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">+6</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">，察觉</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">+8</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">伤害抗性：强酸，寒冷，火焰，闪电，雷鸣</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">感官：盲视</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">60</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">尺，黑暗视觉</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">60</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">尺，被动察觉</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">18</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">语言：史拉蟾语，心灵感应</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">60</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">尺</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">挑战等级：</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">10</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">（</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 华文黑体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">5,900 XP</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 华文黑体; COLOR: rgb(128,0,0); mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: normal; mso-ansi-font-weight: bold">）</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"></span>

FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes';">尺，单一目标。</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'STHeiti light'; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-style: normal; mso-ansi-font-style: italic">命中：</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;
